          <video autoplay="" class="hero-video" id="hero" loop="" muted="" preload="auto">
           <source class="lazy" data-src="/content/dam/BGSU/academics/nursing-rn-bsn/Online-Nursing-Web-1500x900.mp4" src="" type="video/mp4"/>

         <script>
          function initHeroVideo(id, repeat, max){
                    	var queryPath = "video#"+id; 
                    	if($(queryPath)[0] === undefined){
                    		if(repeat <= max){
                        		setTimeout(function(){
                        			initHeroVideo(id);
                        		}, 500);
                    		} else {
                    			if(window.console) console.error("Failed to load video (#"+id+"): timeout max hit");
                    		}
                    	} else {
                    		$(queryPath)[0].load();
                    		setTimeout(function (){
                   		    
                   		     document.getElementById(id).play(); 
                   		    
                   		    }, 1000);
                    	}
                    }
                        $(function() {


                        if (WURFL.is_mobile === true) {
                            //console.log("Mobile Device - show homepage hero image, hide video with no source");
                            	$('div.hidden-phone').hide();
                            	$('.visible-phone').removeClass('visible-phone');

                        }
                        else{
                            //console.log("NOT a mobile device -- move data-src to src");
                            $('source.lazy').each(function(){
									var vidSource = $(this).attr('data-src');
                                    console.log(vidSource);
                                 	$(this).attr({src: vidSource});
                            
                            
                                 	$(this).removeAttr('data-src');


                            }); //Go through EACH video source

                            //$("video#hero")[0].load();
                            initHeroVideo('hero', 0, 10);

                        };
                        




                            var vid = document.getElementById("hero"); 

                            function playVid() { 
                                vid.play(); 
                            }; 

                            function pauseVid() { 
                                vid.pause(); 
                            };



                            $(".home-hero__pause-play.hero").on("click",function() {
                                if ($(this).hasClass('ss-pause')){
                                    pauseVid();
                                    $(this).removeClass('ss-pause').addClass("ss-play").attr("aria-pressed","true").attr("aria-label","play video");
                            
                                }
                                else {
                                    playVid();
                                    $(this).removeClass('ss-play').addClass("ss-pause").attr("aria-pressed","false").attr("aria-label","pause video");
                                };
                            
                            
                            
                            });



    


                            });
         </script>
        </a>
